\section{Class II elimination and immediate BCC linearization}

\section{1. Working microscopic branch}

We start from the explicit Class II working branch
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal L_{\mathrm{mic}}
=
\mathcal L_{\Psi}^{\mathrm{core}}[\Psi]
+
\frac{M_X^2}{2}X_i^a X_i^a
+
\alpha_X X_i^a J_i^a[\Psi]
+
\beta_X X_i^a K_i^a[\Psi].
}
\label{eq:mic_branch_start}
\end{equation}
At the solver-ready level, the nonlinear core is taken as
\begin{equation}
\mathcal L_{\Psi}^{\mathrm{core}}
\leadsto
-\mu^2\Psi
+Z\nabla^2\Psi
-Y\nabla^4\Psi
-\lambda |\Psi|^2\Psi
-\gamma |\Psi|^4\Psi .
\label{eq:core_operator}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Heavy-field elimination}

The algebraic Euler--Lagrange equation for the heavy mediator is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
X_i^a
=
-\frac{1}{M_X^2}
\bigl(
\alpha_X J_i^a+\beta_X K_i^a
\bigr).
}
\label{eq:Xelim_exact}
\end{equation}
Substituting back gives the exact induced effective contribution
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal L_{\mathrm{eff}}^{(X)}
=
-\frac{\alpha_X^2}{2M_X^2}J_i^aJ_i^a
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}J_i^aK_i^a
-\frac{\beta_X^2}{2M_X^2}K_i^aK_i^a.
}
\label{eq:Leff_X_exact}
\end{equation}
The load-bearing mixed term is therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal L_{\mathrm{mix}}^{(II)}
=
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}J_i^aK_i^a.
}
\label{eq:LmixII_exact}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Explicit \texorpdfstring{$\Psi$}{Psi}-only nonlinear PDE}

Use the working promotion
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\rho_\varepsilon:=\Psi^\dagger\Psi+\varepsilon,
\qquad
m^a:=\Psi^\dagger T^a\Psi,
\qquad
n^a:=\frac{m^a}{\rho_\varepsilon},
}
\label{eq:rho_m_n}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
J_i^a=\partial_i m^a,
\qquad
K_i^a=\rho_\varepsilon\,\partial_i n^a
=
\partial_i m^a-n^a\partial_i\rho_\varepsilon.
}
\label{eq:J_K_working}
\end{equation}
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
F_i^a
:=
(\alpha_X+\beta_X)\partial_i m^a
-\beta_X n^a \partial_i\rho_\varepsilon,
}
\label{eq:Fi_def}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
A^a
=
(\alpha_X+\beta_X)T^a\Psi
-\beta_X n^a\Psi,
}
\label{eq:Aa_def}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_i^a
=
(\alpha_X+\beta_X)T^a(\partial_i\Psi)
-\beta_X n^a(\partial_i\Psi)
-\beta_X
\frac{(T^a-n^a\mathbf 1)\Psi}{\rho_\varepsilon}
\,\partial_i\rho_\varepsilon.
}
\label{eq:Bi_def}
\end{equation}
Therefore the exact solver-ready Class II callback is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal G^{(II)}[\Psi]
=
\frac{1}{M_X^2}
\sum_{i,a}
\left[
\partial_i(F_i^aA^a)-F_i^aB_i^a
\right].
}
\label{eq:GII_callback}
\end{equation}
Hence the stationary effective nonlinear PDE is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
-\mu^2\Psi
+Z\nabla^2\Psi
-Y\nabla^4\Psi
-\lambda |\Psi|^2\Psi
-\gamma |\Psi|^4\Psi
+\mathcal G^{(II)}[\Psi]
=0.
}
\label{eq:full_nonlinear_PDE}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Immediate linearization around the BCC locked background}

Take the locked BCC background
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Psi_0(x)=\phi_0(x)\,z_0,
\qquad
z_0^\dagger z_0=1,
\qquad
P_0=z_0z_0^\dagger.
}
\label{eq:BCC_locked_bg}
\end{equation}
Decompose fluctuations as
\begin{equation}
\Psi=\Psi_0+\delta\Psi,
\qquad
\delta\Psi=\sigma z_0+\psi,
\qquad
z_0^\dagger\psi=0,
\label{eq:fluct_split}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\delta P \sim z_0\xi^\dagger+\xi z_0^\dagger,
\qquad
z_0^\dagger\xi=0.
\label{eq:dP_split}
\end{equation}

At the shell-relevant quadratic level, the Class II sector reduces to
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
L_X^{(2)}
=
\frac{M_X^2}{2}X_i^aX_i^a
+
\alpha_X\,m^a X_i^a\,\partial_i\phi_0
+
\beta_X\,X_i^a C_{ij}^{ab}(D_j\psi)\,\xi^b
+\mathrm{h.c.}
}
\label{eq:LX_quadratic_reduced}
\end{equation}
with \(m^a\equiv m^a(P_0)\) and a background-dependent shell tensor \(C_{ij}^{ab}\).

Eliminating \(X_i^a\) again gives
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta L_{\mathrm{enr}}^{(2)}
=
\delta N_{ij}^{\,b}\,
(\partial_i\phi_0)\,
(D_j\psi)\,\xi^b
+\mathrm{h.c.},
}
\label{eq:deltaLenr}
\end{equation}
where the induced Pauli tensor is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta N_{ij}^{\,b}
=
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}\,
m^a\,C_{ij}^{ab}.
}
\label{eq:deltaN_exact}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Explicit shell-adapted Pauli tensor}

Choose the BCC shell-adapted frame
\[
\hat n=\frac{G_*}{|G_*|},
\qquad
(e_1,e_2,\hat n).
\]
For the minimal shell seed
\begin{equation}
m^a=m\,\delta^{a3},
\label{eq:m_seed}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
C_{ij}^{33}=c_\parallel\,\hat n_i\hat n_j,
\label{eq:C33_seed}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
C_{ij}^{31}
=
c_I\,\hat n_i e_{1j}
+
c_J\,\hat n_i e_{2j},
\qquad
C_{ij}^{32}
=
-\,c_J\,\hat n_i e_{1j}
+
c_I\,\hat n_i e_{2j},
\label{eq:C31C32_seed}
\end{equation}
define
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Gamma_X:=\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X\,m}{M_X^2}.
}
\label{eq:GammaX}
\end{equation}
Then the explicit induced Pauli tensor is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
N_{ij}^{3}
=
-\Gamma_X\,c_\parallel\,\hat n_i\hat n_j,
}
\label{eq:N3_explicit}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
N_{ij}^{1}
=
-\Gamma_X
\left(
c_I\,\hat n_i e_{1j}
+
c_J\,\hat n_i e_{2j}
\right),
}
\label{eq:N1_explicit}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
N_{ij}^{2}
=
-\Gamma_X
\left(
-\,c_J\,\hat n_i e_{1j}
+
c_I\,\hat n_i e_{2j}
\right).
}
\label{eq:N2_explicit}
\end{equation}

Thus the shell-adapted transport coefficients at the tensor level are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
g_c^{\rm seed}=-\Gamma_X c_\parallel,
\qquad
g_E^{\rm seed}=-\Gamma_X c_I,
\qquad
g_O^{\rm seed}=-\Gamma_X c_J.
}
\label{eq:gcoeff_seed}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Immediate reduced BCC carrier PDE}

For the explicit defect/BCC profile
\begin{equation}
\theta(\xi)=\theta_0\,\sech(\kappa\xi),
\qquad
f_+(\xi)=\sqrt{\frac{\kappa}{2}}\sech(\kappa\xi),
\qquad
f_-(\xi)=\sqrt{\frac{3\kappa}{2}}\tanh(\kappa\xi)\sech(\kappa\xi),
\label{eq:explicit_profile}
\end{equation}
the exact overlap integrals are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
I_{\theta'^3}
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{256}\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
\qquad
I_\theta
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa.
}
\label{eq:Itheta_exact}
\end{equation}
Hence the reduced coefficients are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\parallel
=
\frac{\lambda_c}{2}I_{\theta'^3}
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{512}\,\lambda_c\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
}
\label{eq:lpar_final}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\alpha
=
I_\theta\,\Lambda_E
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_E,
\qquad
\beta
=
I_\theta\,\Lambda_O
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_O.
}
\label{eq:ab_final}
\end{equation}
Equivalently, at the seed-tensor level,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\parallel
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{512}\,g_c\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
\qquad
\alpha
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,g_E\,\theta_0\kappa,
\qquad
\beta
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,g_O\,\theta_0\kappa.
}
\label{eq:lparab_from_g}
\end{equation}

Therefore the immediate shell-reduced carrier PDE is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Bigl[
i\partial_t
-
\lambda_\parallel\,\sigma_3(-i\partial_\parallel)
-
\alpha\bigl(\sigma_1(-i\partial_{q_1})+\sigma_2(-i\partial_{q_2})\bigr)
-
\beta\bigl(-\sigma_1(-i\partial_{q_2})+\sigma_2(-i\partial_{q_1})\bigr)
\Bigr]\chi=0.
}
\label{eq:reduced_carrier_PDE}
\end{equation}

\section{7. Direct extraction of \texorpdfstring{$W_2,m_*,g_{\mathrm{eff}}$}{W2,m*,g_eff}}

Let \(\chi_\alpha\) be the shell-resolved linearized BCC modes, with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
N_\alpha:=\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2,
}
\label{eq:Nalpha_def}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_\alpha^2
=
u_\alpha^\dagger
\mathcal H_{\rm BCC}(q_0\hat k_\alpha)
u_\alpha,
}
\label{eq:malpha_def}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
g_\alpha
=
\Gamma^{(4)}_{\alpha\alpha\alpha\alpha}(0,0,0,0).
}
\label{eq:galpha_def}
\end{equation}
Then the four raw moments are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
W_0=\sum_{\alpha}N_\alpha,
\qquad
W_2=\sum_{\alpha}N_\alpha\,P_2(\hat n\!\cdot\!\hat k_\alpha),
}
\label{eq:W0W2_def}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
M_2=\sum_{\alpha}N_\alpha\,m_\alpha^2,
\qquad
G_4=\sum_{\alpha}N_\alpha\,g_\alpha.
}
\label{eq:M2G4_def}
\end{equation}
Therefore the extracted microscopic observables are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_*^2=\frac{M_2}{W_0},
\qquad
g_{\mathrm{eff}}=\frac{G_4}{W_0},
\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{lock}}=3\frac{W_2}{W_0}.
}
\label{eq:mstar_geff_epslock}
\end{equation}
Equivalently,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
W_2
=
\sum_{\alpha}
\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2
P_2(\hat n\!\cdot\!\hat k_\alpha),
}
\label{eq:W2_exec_exact}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
M_2
=
\sum_{\alpha}
\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2
u_\alpha^\dagger \mathcal H_{\rm BCC}(q_0\hat k_\alpha)u_\alpha,
}
\label{eq:M2_exec_exact}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
G_4
=
\sum_{\alpha}
\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2
\Gamma^{(4)}_{\alpha\alpha\alpha\alpha}(0,0,0,0).
}
\label{eq:G4_exec_exact}
\end{equation}

\section{8. Leading Class II estimate for the quartic channel}

At diagonal shell projection one has the leading Class II quartic estimate
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
g_\alpha
\sim
\lambda_{\mathrm{eff}}
+
\frac{q_0^2}{M_X^2},
}
\label{eq:galpha_LO}
\end{equation}
hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
g_{\mathrm{eff}}
=
\frac{G_4}{W_0}
\sim
\lambda_{\mathrm{eff}}
+
\frac{q_0^2}{M_X^2}.
}
\label{eq:geff_LO}
\end{equation}

\section{9. Cubic-anisotropy readout}

Once \(W_2,m_*,g_{\mathrm{eff}}\) are extracted, the anisotropy coefficient is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
Z_{\rm cub}
=
-\frac{g_{\mathrm{eff}}^2}{144\pi\,m_*^3}\,
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{lock}}
=
-\frac{G_4^2W_2}{48\pi\,W_0^{3/2}M_2^{3/2}}.
}
\label{eq:Zcub_final}
\end{equation}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\section{Explicit \(OO\) / \(TD+DT\) decomposition of \(\delta J,\delta K\) and the microscopic routing
\(JJ\to\lambda_c,\ JK+KJ\to(\Lambda_E,\Lambda_O)\)}

\section{1. Starting point}

On the current explicit Class II working branch, after eliminating the heavy mediator \(X_i^a\),
the quadratic correction is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_X^{(2)}
=
-\frac{\alpha_X^2}{M_X^2}\,\delta J\,\delta J^\dagger
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}
\bigl(\delta J\,\delta K^\dagger+\delta K\,\delta J^\dagger\bigr)
-\frac{\beta_X^2}{M_X^2}\,\delta K\,\delta K^\dagger.
}
\label{eq:DX2_master_split}
\end{equation}

The exact first variations are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta J_i^a=\partial_i\delta m^a,
}
\label{eq:dJ_master}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta K_i^a
=
\partial_i\!\left[
\frac{1}{\bar\rho}
\bigl(
\delta m^a-\bar q^a\delta\rho
\bigr)
\right]\bar\chi
+
(\partial_i\bar q^a)\,n^\mu D_\mu\psi,
}
\label{eq:dK_master}
\end{equation}
where
\begin{equation}
\bar\rho=|\bar\Psi|^2,
\qquad
\bar m^a=\bar\rho\,\bar q^a.
\end{equation}

We work in the shell-adapted tangent decomposition
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Psi=\phi z,
\qquad
z=
\sqrt{1-|\eta_E|^2-|\eta_O|^2}\,z_0+\eta_E\xi_E+\eta_O\xi_O,
}
\label{eq:z_expand_EO}
\end{equation}
with tangent coefficients
\begin{equation}
c_r^a:=\xi_r^\dagger T^a z_0,
\qquad r\in\{E,O\}.
\end{equation}

To first order,
\begin{equation}
\delta m^a
=
\bar q^a\,\delta\rho
+
\bar\rho\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\,\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\,\bar\eta_r
\bigr).
\label{eq:dm_expand}
\end{equation}
Therefore
\begin{align}
\delta J_i^a
&=
\bar q^a\,\partial_i\delta\rho
+
(\partial_i\bar\rho)\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\,\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\,\bar\eta_r
\bigr)
+
\bar\rho\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\,\partial_i\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\,\partial_i\bar\eta_r
\bigr),
\label{eq:dJ_expand_full}
\\[1mm]
\delta K_i^a
&=
\partial_i\!\left[
\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\,\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\,\bar\eta_r
\bigr)
\right]\bar\chi
+
(\partial_i\bar q^a)\,n^\mu D_\mu\psi
\label{eq:dK_expand_full}
\end{align}
at leading order.

\section{2. \(OO\)-block extraction}

The \(OO\)-block means: keep only the longitudinal scalar fluctuation and suppress the tangent sector,
\begin{equation}
\eta_E=\eta_O=0,
\qquad
\psi=\psi_\parallel.
\end{equation}
Then \eqref{eq:dm_expand} reduces to
\begin{equation}
\delta m^a_{(OO)}=\bar q^a\,\delta\rho.
\label{eq:dm_OO}
\end{equation}
Hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta J_{i,(OO)}^a
=
\bar q^a\,\partial_i\delta\rho.
}
\label{eq:dJ_OO}
\end{equation}

By contrast,
\begin{equation}
\delta m^a_{(OO)}-\bar q^a\delta\rho=0,
\end{equation}
so the first term in \eqref{eq:dK_master} vanishes identically. Moreover the second term is tangent/defect
in nature and does not produce the primitive longitudinal singlet in the present branch.
Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta K_{i,(OO)}^a=0
\qquad\text{at principal longitudinal shell order.}
}
\label{eq:dK_OO_zero}
\end{equation}

Substituting \eqref{eq:dJ_OO}--\eqref{eq:dK_OO_zero} into \eqref{eq:DX2_master_split},
the \(OO\)-block keeps only the pure \(JJ\) term:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta_{OO}^{(2)}
=
-\frac{\alpha_X^2}{M_X^2}\,
\delta J_{(OO)}\,\delta J_{(OO)}^\dagger.
}
\label{eq:OO_reduction}
\end{equation}

After projection to the tangent bundle \(Q_B\), the surviving longitudinal transport density is
\begin{equation}
a_{3;OO}(\xi)
=
\mathfrak P_\parallel[V_{OO}]
=
\frac12\Tr_{Q_B}\!\bigl(\Sigma_3\,n_\mu V^\mu_{OO}(\xi)\bigr).
\label{eq:a3OO_proj}
\end{equation}
Because of the parity filter, the \(\theta'\)-linear term is absent on the current concrete branch,
and the first surviving odd longitudinal term is cubic:
\begin{equation}
a_{3;OO}(\xi)
=
\ell_{0;OO}^{(3)}\,\theta'(\xi)^3+\cdots,
\qquad
\lambda_c=2\,\ell_{0;OO}^{(3)}.
\label{eq:OO_theta3}
\end{equation}
Equivalently,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_c
=
2\lim_{\theta'\to0}
\frac{\mathfrak P_\parallel[V_{OO}]}{\theta'(\xi)^3}.
}
\label{eq:lambdac_limit}
\end{equation}

Thus the \(OO\)-block proves
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
JJ\to\lambda_c,
\qquad
JK,\ KK \not\to \lambda_c
\ \text{at principal order}.
}
\label{eq:OO_routing_final}
\end{equation}

\section{3. \(TD+DT\)-block extraction}

Now keep the tangent sector \((\eta_E,\eta_O)\) and the defect-gradient carrier.
From \eqref{eq:dJ_expand_full}, the tangent part of \(\delta J\) is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta J_{i,(T)}^a
=
(\partial_i\bar\rho)\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\bar\eta_r
\bigr)
+
\bar\rho\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\partial_i\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\partial_i\bar\eta_r
\bigr).
}
\label{eq:dJ_T}
\end{equation}
From \eqref{eq:dK_expand_full},
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta K_{i,(D)}^a
=
\partial_i\!\left[
\sum_{r=E,O}
\bigl(
c_r^a\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\bar\eta_r
\bigr)
\right]\bar\chi
+
(\partial_i\bar q^a)\,n^\mu D_\mu\psi.
}
\label{eq:dK_D}
\end{equation}

These are precisely the mixed shell-gradient / defect-tangent objects.
Hence the projected mixed first-order kernel is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal M^\mu_{TD+DT}
:=
\Pi_Q\bigl(\mathcal V^\mu_{TD}+\mathcal V^\mu_{DT}\bigr)\Pi_Q.
}
\label{eq:MTDDT_def_main}
\end{equation}

At the current branch-level invariant form,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
V^\mu_{TD}
=
\theta'(\xi)\Bigl(
A_E\,E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
A_O\,J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr),
}
\label{eq:VTD_main}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
V^\mu_{DT}
=
\theta'(\xi)\Bigl(
B_E\,E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
B_O\,J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr).
}
\label{eq:VDT_main}
\end{equation}
Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal M^\mu_{TD+DT}
=
\theta'(\xi)\Bigl[
(A_E+B_E)E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
(A_O+B_O)J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr].
}
\label{eq:MTDDT_explicit}
\end{equation}

Applying the invariant projectors,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Lambda_E
=
\mathfrak P_E[\mathcal M_{TD+DT}^{\rm inv}]
=
\frac12(A_E+B_E),
}
\label{eq:LambdaE_read}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Lambda_O
=
\mathfrak P_O[\mathcal M_{TD+DT}^{\rm inv}]
=
\frac12(A_O+B_O).
}
\label{eq:LambdaO_read}
\end{equation}

Thus the mixed block proves
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
JK+KJ\to(\Lambda_E,\Lambda_O).
}
\label{eq:TDDT_routing_final}
\end{equation}

\section{4. Why \(JK+KJ\) and not \(JJ\) or \(KK\) feeds the transverse pair}

Insert the decomposition into \eqref{eq:DX2_master_split}.
The \(JJ\)-piece built from \eqref{eq:dJ_OO} is axial only and gives the longitudinal singlet.
The \(KK\)-piece is purely defect/tangent and remains transverse residual at principal order.
The first term that mixes one shell-gradient/current side with one defect/tangent side is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}
\bigl(
\delta J\,\delta K^\dagger+\delta K\,\delta J^\dagger
\bigr),
}
\label{eq:JK_mixed_source}
\end{equation}
and that is exactly the source of \eqref{eq:MTDDT_explicit}.

Therefore the exact microscopic routing is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
JJ\leftrightarrow OO\text{-longitudinal audit},
\qquad
JK+KJ\leftrightarrow TD+DT\text{-transverse audit},
\qquad
KK\leftrightarrow \text{transverse residual/completion sector}.
}
\label{eq:full_routing_exact}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Reduced PDE dictionary}

Once \(\lambda_c,\Lambda_E,\Lambda_O\) are extracted, the reduced PDE coefficients are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\parallel=\frac{\lambda_c}{2}I_{\theta'^3},
\qquad
\alpha=I_\theta\Lambda_E,
\qquad
\beta=I_\theta\Lambda_O.
}
\label{eq:reduced_dict_main}
\end{equation}
On the explicit seed profile,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
I_{\theta'^3}
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{256}\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
\qquad
I_\theta
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa,
}
\label{eq:seed_overlaps_main}
\end{equation}
so
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\parallel
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{512}\,\lambda_c\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
\qquad
\alpha
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_E,
\qquad
\beta
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_O.
}
\label{eq:reduced_coeffs_main}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Winding asymmetry theorem on the current explicit branch}

The topological defect profile is encoded by the projector path \(P_B(\xi)\), equivalently by
the angular profile \(\theta(\xi)\).
The worldvolume transport kernel is odd because it is built from the defect gradient,
hence every principal transport density carries one odd factor, concretely \(\theta'(\xi)\).

The even/odd transverse tensors are distinguished by the two invariant tangent structures
\[
E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a,
\qquad
J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a.
\]
The \(TD+DT\) principal pair therefore has the decomposition
\begin{equation}
\mathcal M^\mu_{TD+DT}
=
\theta'(\xi)\Bigl[
(A_E+B_E)E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
(A_O+B_O)J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr].
\end{equation}

However, on the explicit odd extra-carrier route the odd channel acquires an additional
winding-sensitive factor:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal I_O
=
X_i^{(O)}\cos\theta(\xi)\,J_jD_j\psi,
}
\label{eq:IO_winding}
\end{equation}
which induces
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
V_{EO}^\mu
=
\theta'(\xi)\cos\theta(\xi)
\Bigl[
\widetilde\Lambda_E\,E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
\widetilde\Lambda_O\,J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr].
}
\label{eq:VEO_winding}
\end{equation}

Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\alpha=\widetilde\Lambda_E\,I_{\theta,\cos},
\qquad
\beta=\widetilde\Lambda_O\,I_{\theta,\cos},
\qquad
I_{\theta,\cos}
=
\int d\xi\,f_+f_-\,\theta'(\xi)\cos\theta(\xi).
}
\label{eq:alpha_beta_Ithetacos}
\end{equation}

Now the asymmetry is this:

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\widetilde\Lambda_O
=
-\frac{\beta_X\gamma_O}{M_X^2}\,C_OJ_1,
}
\label{eq:LambdaO_asym}
\end{equation}
so
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\beta
=
-\frac{\beta_X\gamma_O}{M_X^2}\,C_OJ_1\,I_{\theta,\cos}.
}
\label{eq:beta_asym}
\end{equation}

By contrast, the even coefficient has no independent odd-overlap invariant \(J_1\):
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\alpha=\widetilde\Lambda_E\,I_{\theta,\cos},
}
\label{eq:alpha_asym}
\end{equation}
with \(\widetilde\Lambda_E\) read from the \(E\)-projector channel.

Hence, within the present explicit branch, the topological winding contributes \emph{asymmetrically} as follows:

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\text{even branch: }
\Lambda_E\ \text{is controlled by the }E\text{-projected carrier amplitude;}
}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\text{odd branch: }
\Lambda_O\ \text{is controlled by the }J\text{-projected carrier amplitude}
\ \times\ \text{the oriented overlap }J_1.
}
\end{equation}

Equivalently, the odd coefficient is sign-sensitive to the winding/overlap orientation:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\operatorname{sgn}\beta
=
-\operatorname{sgn}\!\bigl(\beta_X\gamma_O\,C_OJ_1\,I_{\theta,\cos}\bigr).
}
\label{eq:beta_sign_winding}
\end{equation}

Therefore the BCC/defect winding does \emph{not} enter \(\Lambda_E\) and \(\Lambda_O\) symmetrically.
It enters the odd channel through the oriented \(J\)-overlap invariant \(J_1\), while the even channel is read from the non-odd \(E\)-projector channel.
This is the precise microscopic origin of the \(\Lambda_E/\Lambda_O\) asymmetry on the current explicit mixed/odd-completion route.

\section{7. Final theorem on the current working branch}

Combining everything, on the present explicit Class II working branch we have
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta J,\delta K
=
(\delta J,\delta K)_{OO}
+
(\delta J,\delta K)_{TD+DT}
+
(\delta J,\delta K)_{\rm rem},
}
\end{equation}
with
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(\delta J,\delta K)_{OO}:
\quad
\delta J_{i,(OO)}^a=\bar q^a\partial_i\delta\rho,
\qquad
\delta K_{i,(OO)}^a=0
\ \text{(principal order),}
}
\end{equation}
and
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(\delta J,\delta K)_{TD+DT}:
\quad
\delta J_{i,(T)}^a,\ \delta K_{i,(D)}^a
\ \text{given by \eqref{eq:dJ_T}, \eqref{eq:dK_D}.}
}
\end{equation}

Therefore
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
JJ\to\lambda_c,
\qquad
JK+KJ\to(\Lambda_E,\Lambda_O),
\qquad
KK\to\text{residual}.
}
\end{equation}

After overlap insertion,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\lambda_\parallel
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{512}\,\lambda_c\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
\qquad
\alpha
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_E,
\qquad
\beta
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_O.
}
\end{equation}

And on the explicit odd route,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\beta
=
-\frac{\beta_X\gamma_O}{M_X^2}\,C_OJ_1\,I_{\theta,\cos},
}
\end{equation}
so the odd coefficient is explicitly winding/orientation sensitive, whereas the even coefficient is not controlled by the same odd-overlap invariant.
This is the desired asymmetric winding contribution.

\section{Final Summary}

On the current explicit Class II working branch, the first variations split as
\[
\delta J_i^a=\partial_i\delta m^a,
\qquad
\delta K_i^a
=
\partial_i\!\left[
\frac{1}{\bar\rho}
(\delta m^a-\bar q^a\delta\rho)
\right]\bar\chi
+
(\partial_i\bar q^a)\,n^\mu D_\mu\psi.
\]

For the \(OO\)-sector,
\[
\delta m^a_{(OO)}=\bar q^a\delta\rho,
\qquad
\delta J_{i,(OO)}^a=\bar q^a\partial_i\delta\rho,
\qquad
\delta K_{i,(OO)}^a=0
\quad\text{at principal order}.
\]
Hence
\[
JJ\to OO\to \lambda_c,
\qquad
\lambda_c
=
2\lim_{\theta'\to0}
\frac{\mathfrak P_\parallel[V_{OO}]}{\theta'(\xi)^3}.
\]

For the mixed shell--defect sector,
\[
\delta J_{i,(T)}^a
=
(\partial_i\bar\rho)\sum_{r=E,O}
(c_r^a\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\bar\eta_r)
+
\bar\rho\sum_{r=E,O}
(c_r^a\partial_i\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\partial_i\bar\eta_r),
\]
\[
\delta K_{i,(D)}^a
=
\partial_i\!\left[
\sum_{r=E,O}(c_r^a\eta_r+\bar c_r^a\bar\eta_r)
\right]\bar\chi
+
(\partial_i\bar q^a)\,n^\mu D_\mu\psi.
\]
Therefore
\[
JK+KJ\to TD+DT\to (\Lambda_E,\Lambda_O),
\]
with
\[
\mathcal M^\mu_{TD+DT}
=
\theta'(\xi)\Bigl[
(A_E+B_E)E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
(A_O+B_O)J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr],
\]
\[
\Lambda_E=\frac12(A_E+B_E),
\qquad
\Lambda_O=\frac12(A_O+B_O).
\]

After overlap insertion,
\[
\lambda_\parallel
=
-\frac{3\sqrt3\pi}{512}\,\lambda_c\,\theta_0^3\kappa^3,
\qquad
\alpha
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_E,
\qquad
\beta
=
-\frac{\sqrt3\pi}{16}\,\theta_0\kappa\,\Lambda_O.
\]

The winding asymmetry is explicit on the odd route:
\[
V_{EO}^\mu
=
\theta'(\xi)\cos\theta(\xi)
\Bigl[
\widetilde\Lambda_E E^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
+
\widetilde\Lambda_O J^\mu{}_a\Sigma_a
\Bigr],
\]
\[
\widetilde\Lambda_O
=
-\frac{\beta_X\gamma_O}{M_X^2}\,C_OJ_1,
\qquad
\beta
=
-\frac{\beta_X\gamma_O}{M_X^2}\,C_OJ_1\,I_{\theta,\cos},
\qquad
I_{\theta,\cos}
=
\int d\xi\,f_+f_-\,\theta'(\xi)\cos\theta(\xi).
\]

Thus the odd coefficient carries the oriented overlap invariant \(J_1\), while the even coefficient does not.
Hence the topological winding contributes asymmetrically to \(\Lambda_E\) and \(\Lambda_O\) on the present explicit branch.

\section{Closed numerical status on the frozen corrected branch}

\section{1. Frozen corrected seed}

The corrected seed is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\delta_{\mathrm{corr}}=(\delta_A,\delta_E,\delta_O)=(0.0096,-0.0288,0.0096).
}
\end{equation}

\section{2. Exact fast six-row Hessian values in the minimal rigid-internal first-shell truncation}

In the minimal rigid-internal first-shell truncation,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Psi(x)=\phi(x)\,z_0,
\qquad
\partial_iP=0,
\qquad
K_A=K_E=K_O=0.
}
\end{equation}
Therefore all fast quadratic response coefficients vanish identically:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{AA}
=
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{EE}
=
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{OO}
=
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{AE}
=
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{AO}
=
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{EO}
=
0.
}
\end{equation}

Hence
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
Q_2(\delta_{\mathrm{corr}})=0,
\qquad
\beta^{\mathrm{corr}}=0.
}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Consequence for the transverse tensor pair}

At branch-level reduced summary,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Lambda_E^{\mathrm{pr}}=\frac12(A_E+B_E),
\qquad
\Lambda_O^{\mathrm{pr}}=\frac12(A_O+B_O).
}
\end{equation}
Since the fast transverse sector vanishes in the above truncation, the only numerically forced result is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
A_E+B_E=0,
\qquad
A_O+B_O=0.
}
\end{equation}

Accordingly,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\alpha_{\mathrm{pr}}=0,
\qquad
\beta_{\mathrm{pr}}=0
}
\end{equation}
within this minimal truncation.

\section{4. What cannot be honestly extracted yet}

The individual numbers
\[
A_E,\quad B_E,\quad A_O,\quad B_O
\]
are not determined by the currently uploaded data, because the notes explicitly state that their literal blockwise Hessian differentiation and projection on the intended branch still remain to be done.

Likewise, the actual branch values of
\[
m_*^2=\frac{M_2}{W_0},
\qquad
g_{\mathrm{eff}}=\frac{G_4}{W_0}
\]
cannot yet be evaluated numerically from the uploaded data alone, because the raw moments
\[
W_0,\quad W_2,\quad M_2,\quad G_4
\]
have not yet been extracted from the actual intended-branch outputs.

Therefore the honest numerical status is:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H^{(2)}_{rs}=0\ \text{for all }r,s\in\{A,E,O\}
\quad\text{(minimal fast truncation)},
}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
A_E+B_E=0,\qquad A_O+B_O=0,
}
\end{equation}
but
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
A_E,\ B_E,\ A_O,\ B_O,\ m_*,\ g_{\mathrm{eff}}
\ \text{are not uniquely numerically fixed by the currently uploaded data.}
}
\end{equation}

\section{Final Honest Numerical Summary}

For the frozen corrected branch
\[
\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}
=
\Psi_{\mathrm{BCC}}
+
0.0096\,\Phi_A
-
0.0288\,\Phi_E
+
0.0096\,\Phi_O,
\]
the currently uploaded notes allow a fully honest numerical closure only at the level of the minimal rigid-internal first-shell truncation.

In that truncation,
\[
\partial_iP=0,
\qquad
K_A=K_E=K_O=0,
\]
hence
\[
\boxed{
H^{(2)}_{AA}
=
H^{(2)}_{EE}
=
H^{(2)}_{OO}
=
H^{(2)}_{AE}
=
H^{(2)}_{AO}
=
H^{(2)}_{EO}
=
0.
}
\]

Therefore
\[
\boxed{
Q_2(\delta_{\mathrm{corr}})=0,
\qquad
\beta^{\mathrm{corr}}=0.
}
\]

At the principal transverse summary level,
\[
\Lambda_E^{\mathrm{pr}}=\frac12(A_E+B_E),
\qquad
\Lambda_O^{\mathrm{pr}}=\frac12(A_O+B_O),
\]
so the only numerically forced result is
\[
\boxed{
A_E+B_E=0,
\qquad
A_O+B_O=0.
}
\]

However, the individual numbers
\[
A_E,\quad B_E,\quad A_O,\quad B_O
\]
are not yet uniquely fixed by the uploaded data, because the notes explicitly state that their literal blockwise Hessian differentiation on the intended branch remains open.

Likewise, the exact intended-branch observables

m_*^2=\frac{M_2}{W_0},
\qquad

So the final honest numerical status is:

\ \text{for all }r,s\in\{A,E,O\}
\quad\text{(minimal fast truncation),}

\section{Complete Numerical Algorithm for
\texorpdfstring{$\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}\to \bar A_G \to (W_0,W_2,M_2,G_4)\to (m_*,g_{\mathrm{eff}})$}{Psi_corr to bar A_G to raw moments to m* and g_eff}}

\section{1. Inputs}

We assume that a numerically accepted stationary branch
\[
\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}(x)
=
\Psi_{\mathrm{BCC}}(x)
+
0.0096\,\Phi_A(x)
-
0.0288\,\Phi_E(x)
+
0.0096\,\Phi_O(x)
\]
is already available on a periodic box \(\Omega=[0,L)^3\) sampled on an \(N_x\times N_y\times N_z\) grid.

The algorithm takes as input:

\begin{enumerate}
\item the complex triplet field \(\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}(x)\in\mathbb C^3\);
\item the selected shell radius \(q_0\);
\item the selected reciprocal shell \(S_*=\{G\}\);
\item the patch centers \(\{\hat k_\alpha\}_{\alpha=1}^{N_{\rm patch}}\) on the shell;
\item the anisotropy axis \(\hat n\);
\item the family projector \(\Pi_{\rm fam}\);
\item the microscopic residual operator \(R[\Psi]\) or equivalently the shell free energy \(\mathcal F_{\rm shell}\).
\end{enumerate}

\section{2. Fourier extraction of the frozen harmonics}

Define the Fourier coefficients of the accepted branch by
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\bar A_G
=
\frac{1}{|\Omega|}
\int_\Omega d^3x\;
e^{-iG\cdot x}\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}(x).
}
\label{eq:barAG_def_alg}
\end{equation}

If the orbit tangent fields \(\Phi_r\) (\(r\in\{A,E,O\}\)) are known explicitly, define
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
B_G^{(r)}
=
\frac{1}{|\Omega|}
\int_\Omega d^3x\;
e^{-iG\cdot x}\Phi_r(x).
}
\label{eq:BGr_def_alg}
\end{equation}

If \(\Phi_r\) is not stored explicitly, reconstruct it numerically from branch derivatives:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Phi_r
=
\frac{\partial \Psi(\delta_A,\delta_E,\delta_O)}{\partial \delta_r}
\Bigg|_{\delta=(0.0096,-0.0288,0.0096)}.
}
\label{eq:Phi_from_branch_derivative}
\end{equation}
A central-difference implementation is
\begin{equation}
\Phi_r
\approx
\frac{
\Psi(\delta+h\,e_r)-\Psi(\delta-h\,e_r)
}{2h}.
\label{eq:Phi_central_diff}
\end{equation}

\section{3. Harmonic-level construction of the fast six-row sector}

For each orbit direction \(r\in\{A,E,O\}\), define
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
N_r(x)=\bar\Psi^\dagger\Phi_r+\Phi_r^\dagger\bar\Psi,
}
\label{eq:Nr_x_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
M_r^a(x)=\bar\Psi^\dagger T^a\Phi_r+\Phi_r^\dagger T^a\bar\Psi,
}
\label{eq:Mr_x_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
Q_r^a(x)=\frac{M_r^a(x)-\bar q^a(x)N_r(x)}{\bar\rho(x)},
\qquad
\bar\rho=\bar\Psi^\dagger\bar\Psi,
\qquad
\bar q^a=\frac{\bar\Psi^\dagger T^a\bar\Psi}{\bar\rho}.
}
\label{eq:Qr_x_alg}
\end{equation}

Define also the shell-normal carrier derivative
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\chi_r(x)=n^\mu D_\mu \Phi_r(x).
}
\label{eq:chir_x_alg}
\end{equation}

In Fourier space these become finite convolutions:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\widehat N_r(Q)
=
\sum_G
\Bigl(
\bar A_G^\dagger B_{G+Q}^{(r)}
+
B_G^{(r)\dagger}\bar A_{G+Q}
\Bigr),
}
\label{eq:Nhat_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\widehat M_r^a(Q)
=
\sum_G
\Bigl(
\bar A_G^\dagger T^a B_{G+Q}^{(r)}
+
B_G^{(r)\dagger}T^a\bar A_{G+Q}
\Bigr),
}
\label{eq:Mhat_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\widehat J_{r,i}^a(Q)=iQ_i\,\widehat M_r^a(Q),
}
\label{eq:Jhat_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\widehat K_{r,i}^a(Q)
=
iQ_i\,\widehat Q_r^a(Q)\,\bar\chi
+
(\partial_i\bar q^a)\widehat\chi_r(Q).
}
\label{eq:Khat_alg}
\end{equation}

Then all six fast coefficients are computed from the single common overlap formula
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{rs}
=
-\frac{\alpha_X\beta_X}{M_X^2}
\mathfrak P_O
\left[
\sum_Q \widehat J_{r,i}^a(Q)\widehat K_{s,i}^a(-Q)^\dagger
+
\sum_Q \widehat J_{s,i}^a(Q)\widehat K_{r,i}^a(-Q)^\dagger
+\mathrm{h.c.}
\right].
}
\label{eq:H2fast_alg}
\end{equation}

This completes the \(\bar A_G\)-to-\(H^{(2)}_{rs}\) part of the extractor.

\section{4. Patch projectors on the accepted shell}

To extract the raw moments, define a shell-band projector and patch projectors.

The shell-band projector is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(\mathcal P_{\rm shell}f)\widehat{\ }(k)
=
\mathbf 1_{\{|\,|k|-q_0\,|<\Delta q\}}
\hat f(k).
}
\label{eq:Pshell_alg}
\end{equation}

For each patch center \(\hat k_\alpha\), define
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
(\mathcal P_\alpha f)\widehat{\ }(k)
=
\mathbf 1_{\{|\,|k|-q_0\,|<\Delta q\}}
\mathbf 1_{\{\arccos(\hat k\cdot\hat k_\alpha)<\Delta\theta\}}
\hat f(k).
}
\label{eq:Palpha_alg}
\end{equation}

The family-projected patch space is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal H_\alpha
=
\Pi_{\rm fam}\,\mathcal P_\alpha\,\mathcal H.
}
\label{eq:Halpha_alg}
\end{equation}

\section{5. Matrix-free Hessian on the accepted branch}

Let \(R[\Psi]\) denote the stationary PDE residual:
\begin{equation}
R[\Psi]=0
\quad\text{at}\quad
\Psi=\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}.
\end{equation}

Define the Jacobian/Hessian-vector product by central difference:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal H[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}]\cdot v
\approx
\frac{R[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}+\varepsilon v]-R[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}-\varepsilon v]}{2\varepsilon}.
}
\label{eq:Hessian_vec_alg}
\end{equation}

Equivalently, if the shell free energy \(\mathcal F_{\rm shell}\) is available,
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal H[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}]
=
\frac{\delta^2 \mathcal F_{\rm shell}}{\delta\bar\Psi\,\delta\Psi}
\Bigg|_{\Psi=\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}}.
}
\label{eq:Hessian_energy_alg}
\end{equation}

\section{6. Extraction of \texorpdfstring{$\chi_\alpha$}{chi alpha} and \texorpdfstring{$m_\alpha^2$}{m alpha squared}}

For each patch \(\alpha\), restrict the Hessian to \(\mathcal H_\alpha\):
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal H_\alpha^{\rm proj}
=
\mathcal P_\alpha \Pi_{\rm fam}\,
\mathcal H[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}]\,
\Pi_{\rm fam}\mathcal P_\alpha.
}
\label{eq:Halpha_proj}
\end{equation}

Compute its lowest relevant normalized eigenvector and eigenvalue:
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\mathcal H_\alpha^{\rm proj}\chi_\alpha
=
m_\alpha^2\,\chi_\alpha,
\qquad
\|\chi_\alpha\|=1.
}
\label{eq:chi_alpha_eig}
\end{equation}

Then define the patch weight
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
N_\alpha
=
\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2.
}
\label{eq:Nalpha_alg}
\end{equation}

In exact projected notation, this is the same object as
\begin{equation}
N_\alpha=\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2,
\qquad
m_\alpha^2=u_\alpha^\dagger H_{\rm BCC}(q_0\hat k_\alpha)u_\alpha.
\end{equation}

\section{7. Extraction of the diagonal quartic vertex \texorpdfstring{$g_\alpha$}{g alpha}}

There are two equivalent numerical routes.

\subsection{Route A: direct four-point derivative}

Define a normalized patch mode \(\varphi_\alpha=\chi_\alpha/\|\chi_\alpha\|\).
Then
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
g_\alpha
=
\Gamma^{(4)}_{\alpha\alpha\alpha\alpha}(0,0,0,0)
=
\frac{\partial^4}{\partial h^4}
\mathcal F_{\rm shell}[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}+h\varphi_\alpha]
\Bigg|_{h=0}\Big/12.
}
\label{eq:galpha_direct_alg}
\end{equation}

A symmetric five-point stencil gives
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
g_\alpha
\approx
\frac{
F_\alpha(-2h)-4F_\alpha(-h)+6F_\alpha(0)-4F_\alpha(h)+F_\alpha(2h)
}{12h^4},
}
\label{eq:galpha_fd_alg}
\end{equation}
where
\[
F_\alpha(h):=\mathcal F_{\rm shell}[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}+h\varphi_\alpha].
\]

\subsection{Route B: quadratic--quartic fit}

For small real amplitudes \(h_j\), evaluate
\begin{equation}
\Delta F_\alpha(h_j)
=
\mathcal F_{\rm shell}[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}+h_j\varphi_\alpha]
-
\mathcal F_{\rm shell}[\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}].
\end{equation}
Fit
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Delta F_\alpha(h)
=
m_\alpha^2 h^2
+
\frac{g_\alpha}{2}h^4
+
O(h^6).
}
\label{eq:quartic_fit_alg}
\end{equation}
Then the fitted quartic coefficient is \(g_\alpha\).

\section{8. Raw moments}

Once \((N_\alpha,m_\alpha^2,g_\alpha)\) are available for all patches,
define
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
W_0=\sum_{\alpha=1}^{N_{\rm patch}}N_\alpha,
}
\label{eq:W0_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
W_2=\sum_{\alpha=1}^{N_{\rm patch}}N_\alpha\,P_2(\hat n\cdot\hat k_\alpha),
\qquad
P_2(c)=\frac12(3c^2-1),
}
\label{eq:W2_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
M_2=\sum_{\alpha=1}^{N_{\rm patch}}N_\alpha\,m_\alpha^2,
}
\label{eq:M2_alg}
\end{equation}
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
G_4=\sum_{\alpha=1}^{N_{\rm patch}}N_\alpha\,g_\alpha.
}
\label{eq:G4_alg}
\end{equation}

\section{9. Final evaluator}

The effective observables are
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_*^2=\frac{M_2}{W_0},
\qquad
m_*=\sqrt{\frac{M_2}{W_0}},
\qquad
g_{\mathrm{eff}}=\frac{G_4}{W_0},
\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{lock}}=3\frac{W_2}{W_0}.
}
\label{eq:final_eval_alg}
\end{equation}

The cubic anisotropy coefficient is
\begin{equation}
\boxed{
Z_{\rm cub}
=
-\frac{G_4^2W_2}{48\pi\,W_0^{3/2}M_2^{3/2}}
=
-\frac{g_{\mathrm{eff}}^2}{144\pi\,m_*^3}\,\varepsilon_{\mathrm{lock}}.
}
\label{eq:Zcub_alg}
\end{equation}

\section{10. Acceptance and numerical stability checks}

A numerically honest run must verify:

\begin{enumerate}
\item grid convergence in \((N_x,N_y,N_z)\);
\item box-size convergence in \(L\);
\item shell-band tolerance stability in \((\Delta q,\Delta\theta)\);
\item Hessian-vector stability in \(\varepsilon\);
\item quartic-fit stability in \(h\);
\item patch-count stability in \(N_{\rm patch}\);
\item positivity conditions
\[
W_0>0,\qquad M_2>0.
\]
\end{enumerate}

Only after these checks should the run be accepted as the actual intended-branch numerical output.

\begin{verbatim}

import numpy as np
from numpy.fft import fftn, ifftn, fftfreq
from scipy.sparse.linalg import eigsh, LinearOperator

# ============================================================
# 0. USER-SUPPLIED OBJECTS
# ============================================================
# Psi_corr          : accepted stationary branch, shape (3, Nx, Ny, Nz), complex
# q0                : selected shell radius
# hat_n             : anisotropy axis, shape (3,)
# patch_centers     : array of patch unit vectors hat{k}_alpha, shape (Npatch, 3)
# T_list            : generators T^a, list of 3x3 complex matrices
# Pi_fam_apply(v)   : family projector action on field v
# residual(Psi)     : stationary PDE residual R[Psi]
# shell_free_energy(Psi) : shell free energy F_shell[Psi]
# optional:
#   Phi_orbit = {"A": Phi_A, "E": Phi_E, "O": Phi_O}
#   or branch_solver(deltaA, deltaE, deltaO) -> Psi(delta)
# ============================================================

# -------------------------
# numerical knobs
# -------------------------
dq = 0.08 * q0
dtheta = 0.35
eps_hess = 1e-6
h_quartic = 5e-4
real_dtype = np.float64
complex_dtype = np.complex128

# ============================================================
# 1. FFT / reciprocal grid
# ============================================================
def make_kgrid(Nx, Ny, Nz, Lx, Ly, Lz):
    kx = 2*np.pi*fftfreq(Nx, d=Lx/Nx)
    ky = 2*np.pi*fftfreq(Ny, d=Ly/Ny)
    kz = 2*np.pi*fftfreq(Nz, d=Lz/Nz)
    KX, KY, KZ = np.meshgrid(kx, ky, kz, indexing='ij')
    K = np.stack([KX, KY, KZ], axis=0)
    Kmag = np.sqrt(np.sum(K**2, axis=0))
    return K, Kmag

def fft_field(Psi):
    return fftn(Psi, axes=(1,2,3))

def ifft_field(Psi_k):
    return ifftn(Psi_k, axes=(1,2,3))

# ============================================================
# 2. extract frozen shell harmonics \bar A_G
# ============================================================
def extract_shell_harmonics(Psi_corr, G_list, xgrid=None):
    """
    Returns dict: G_tuple -> barA_G (complex 3-vector)
    Assumes G_list exactly matches reciprocal-grid frequencies.
    """
    Psi_k = fft_field(Psi_corr)
    barA = {}
    for G in G_list:
        idx = reciprocal_index_from_vector(G, Psi_k.shape[1:])  # user-defined lookup
        # FFT normalization must be consistent across the whole codebase
        barA[tuple(np.round(G, 12))] = Psi_k[:, idx[0], idx[1], idx[2]] / np.prod(Psi_k.shape[1:])
    return barA

# ============================================================
# 3. orbit tangent fields Phi_r and their harmonics B_G^(r)
# ============================================================
def central_branch_derivative(branch_solver, delta_vec, r, h):
    d = np.zeros(3)
    d[r] = h
    Psi_p = branch_solver(*(delta_vec + d))
    Psi_m = branch_solver(*(delta_vec - d))
    return (Psi_p - Psi_m) / (2*h)

def extract_orbit_fields_and_harmonics(delta_vec, G_list, Phi_orbit=None, branch_solver=None, h=1e-4):
    out = {}
    labels = ["A", "E", "O"]
    for ir, label in enumerate(labels):
        if Phi_orbit is not None:
            Phi = Phi_orbit[label]
        else:
            Phi = central_branch_derivative(branch_solver, np.array(delta_vec), ir, h)
        B = extract_shell_harmonics(Phi, G_list)
        out[label] = {"Phi": Phi, "B": B}
    return out

# ============================================================
# 4. harmonic convolutions for N_r, M_r^a, Q_r, chi_r, J_r, K_r
# ============================================================
def compute_background_fields(Psi_corr, T_list, K, grad_operator):
    rho = np.sum(np.conj(Psi_corr) * Psi_corr, axis=0).real
    q = []
    for T in T_list:
        TPsi = np.einsum('ab,bxyz->axyz', T, Psi_corr)
        num = np.sum(np.conj(Psi_corr) * TPsi, axis=0)
        q.append(num / (rho + 1e-14))
    q = np.array(q)  # shape (na, Nx, Ny, Nz)
    grad_q = grad_operator(q)  # user-defined: returns shape (3, na, Nx, Ny, Nz)
    return rho, q, grad_q

def harmonic_convolution(barA, B_r, T_list, all_Q):
    """
    barA: dict G -> 3-vector
    B_r : dict G -> 3-vector
    Returns Nhat[Q], Mhat[a,Q]
    """
    Nhat = {}
    Mhat = {a: {} for a in range(len(T_list))}
    G_keys = list(barA.keys())

    for Q in all_Q:
        Qk = tuple(np.round(Q, 12))
        Nsum = 0.0 + 0.0j
        Msum = [0.0 + 0.0j for _ in range(len(T_list))]
        for Gk in G_keys:
            G = np.array(Gk)
            GpQ = tuple(np.round(G + Q, 12))
            if GpQ not in B_r:
                continue
            aG = barA[Gk]
            bGQ = B_r[GpQ]
            if Gk in B_r and GpQ in barA:
                bG = B_r[Gk]
                aGQ = barA[GpQ]
            else:
                bG = None
                aGQ = None

            Nsum += np.vdot(aG, bGQ)
            if (bG is not None) and (aGQ is not None):
                Nsum += np.vdot(bG, aGQ)

            for ia, T in enumerate(T_list):
                Msum[ia] += np.vdot(aG, T @ bGQ)
                if (bG is not None) and (aGQ is not None):
                    Msum[ia] += np.vdot(bG, T @ aGQ)

        Nhat[Qk] = Nsum
        for ia in range(len(T_list)):
            Mhat[ia][Qk] = Msum[ia]
    return Nhat, Mhat

def compute_JK_harmonics(Nhat, Mhat, qbar_hat, chibar_hat, grad_qbar_x, all_Q):
    Jhat = {}
    Khat = {}
    for Q in all_Q:
        Qk = tuple(np.round(Q, 12))
        Qvec = np.array(Q)
        for ia in Mhat:
            for i in range(3):
                Jhat[(ia, i, Qk)] = 1j * Qvec[i] * Mhat[ia][Qk]
                # user must define Qhat from Mhat and Nhat consistently with background rho_hat
                Qhat_val = compute_Qhat_from_Mhat_Nhat(Mhat[ia][Qk], Nhat[Qk], qbar_hat[ia][Qk])
                Khat[(ia, i, Qk)] = 1j * Qvec[i] * Qhat_val * chibar_hat[Qk] \
                                  + grad_qbar_x[i, ia] * compute_chi_r_hat(Qk)
    return Jhat, Khat

def compute_H2_fast(Jhat_r, Khat_s, alpha_X, beta_X, M_X, odd_projector):
    total = 0.0 + 0.0j
    for key in Jhat_r:
        ia, i, Qk = key
        minusQ = tuple(np.round(-np.array(Qk), 12))
        if (ia, i, minusQ) not in Khat_s:
            continue
        total += Jhat_r[(ia, i, Qk)] * np.conj(Khat_s[(ia, i, minusQ)])
    total = total + np.conj(total)
    return -(alpha_X * beta_X / (M_X**2)) * odd_projector(total)

# ============================================================
# 5. patch projectors
# ============================================================
def patch_mask(K, Kmag, q0, hat_k_alpha, dq, dtheta):
    kmag_ok = np.abs(Kmag - q0) < dq
    Khat = K / (Kmag[None, ...] + 1e-14)
    cosang = np.sum(Khat * hat_k_alpha[:, None, None, None], axis=0)
    ang_ok = np.arccos(np.clip(cosang, -1.0, 1.0)) < dtheta
    return kmag_ok & ang_ok

def project_patch(v, mask):
    vk = fft_field(v)
    vk = vk * mask[None, ...]
    return ifft_field(vk)

# ============================================================
# 6. matrix-free Hessian-vector product at Psi_corr
# ============================================================
def hessian_vec(Psi_corr, v, residual, eps=1e-6):
    Rp = residual(Psi_corr + eps*v)
    Rm = residual(Psi_corr - eps*v)
    return (Rp - Rm) / (2*eps)

# ============================================================
# 7. projected eigenmode extraction per patch
# ============================================================
def flatten_complex_field(v):
    return np.concatenate([v.real.ravel(), v.imag.ravel()])

def unflatten_complex_field(x, shape):
    n = np.prod(shape)
    re = x[:n].reshape(shape)
    im = x[n:].reshape(shape)
    return re + 1j*im

def build_patch_linear_operator(Psi_corr, patch_mask_alpha, Pi_fam_apply, residual):
    shape = Psi_corr.shape
    size = 2 * np.prod(shape)

    def mv(x):
        v = unflatten_complex_field(x, shape)
        v = project_patch(Pi_fam_apply(v), patch_mask_alpha)
        Hv = hessian_vec(Psi_corr, v, residual, eps=eps_hess)
        Hv = project_patch(Pi_fam_apply(Hv), patch_mask_alpha)
        return flatten_complex_field(Hv)

    return LinearOperator((size, size), matvec=mv, dtype=np.float64)

def extract_patch_mode(Psi_corr, patch_mask_alpha, Pi_fam_apply, residual):
    Lop = build_patch_linear_operator(Psi_corr, patch_mask_alpha, Pi_fam_apply, residual)
    evals, evecs = eigsh(Lop, k=4, which='SM')   # smallest-magnitude / user-adjust as needed
    idx = np.argmin(np.abs(evals))
    chi = unflatten_complex_field(evecs[:, idx], Psi_corr.shape)
    chi = project_patch(Pi_fam_apply(chi), patch_mask_alpha)
    norm = np.sqrt(np.sum(np.abs(chi)**2))
    chi /= (norm + 1e-14)
    m2 = float(evals[idx].real)
    Nalpha = float(np.sum(np.abs(Pi_fam_apply(chi))**2).real)
    return chi, m2, Nalpha

# ============================================================
# 8. quartic coefficient g_alpha
# ============================================================
def extract_galpha_from_energy(Psi_corr, chi_alpha, shell_free_energy, h=5e-4):
    def F(t):
        return shell_free_energy(Psi_corr + t * chi_alpha)

    Fm2 = F(-2*h)
    Fm1 = F(-h)
    F0  = F(0.0)
    Fp1 = F(h)
    Fp2 = F(2*h)

    fourth_deriv = (Fm2 - 4*Fm1 + 6*F0 - 4*Fp1 + Fp2) / (h**4)
    g_alpha = fourth_deriv / 12.0
    return float(np.real(g_alpha))

# ============================================================
# 9. raw moments and final outputs
# ============================================================
def P2(c):
    return 0.5 * (3*c*c - 1.0)

def compute_raw_moments(hat_n, patch_centers, N_list, m2_list, g_list):
    W0 = 0.0
    W2 = 0.0
    M2 = 0.0
    G4 = 0.0

    for hat_k, Nalpha, m2, galpha in zip(patch_centers, N_list, m2_list, g_list):
        c = float(np.dot(hat_n, hat_k))
        p2 = P2(c)
        W0 += Nalpha
        W2 += Nalpha * p2
        M2 += Nalpha * m2
        G4 += Nalpha * galpha

    return W0, W2, M2, G4

def compute_effective_observables(W0, W2, M2, G4):
    mstar2 = M2 / W0
    mstar = np.sqrt(mstar2)
    geff = G4 / W0
    eps_lock = 3.0 * W2 / W0
    Zcub = -(G4**2 * W2) / (48.0 * np.pi * (W0**1.5) * (M2**1.5))
    return dict(mstar2=mstar2, mstar=mstar, geff=geff, eps_lock=eps_lock, Zcub=Zcub)

# ============================================================
# 10. master pipeline
# ============================================================
def full_actual_branch_extractor(Psi_corr, q0, hat_n, patch_centers, K, Kmag,
                                 Pi_fam_apply, residual, shell_free_energy):
    N_list, m2_list, g_list = [], [], []

    for hat_k_alpha in patch_centers:
        mask = patch_mask(K, Kmag, q0, hat_k_alpha, dq=dq, dtheta=dtheta)
        chi_alpha, m2, Nalpha = extract_patch_mode(Psi_corr, mask, Pi_fam_apply, residual)
        galpha = extract_galpha_from_energy(Psi_corr, chi_alpha, shell_free_energy, h=h_quartic)

        N_list.append(Nalpha)
        m2_list.append(m2)
        g_list.append(galpha)

    W0, W2, M2, G4 = compute_raw_moments(hat_n, patch_centers, N_list, m2_list, g_list)
    obs = compute_effective_observables(W0, W2, M2, G4)

    return {
        "N_alpha": np.array(N_list),
        "m_alpha2": np.array(m2_list),
        "g_alpha": np.array(g_list),
        "W0": W0,
        "W2": W2,
        "M2": M2,
        "G4": G4,
        **obs
    }
\end{verbatim}

\section{Final Summary}

The complete numerical extraction pipeline from the accepted corrected branch is:

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}
\;\xrightarrow{\text{FFT}}\;
\bar A_G
\;\xrightarrow{\text{orbit tangents}}\;
B_G^{(A)},B_G^{(E)},B_G^{(O)}
\;\xrightarrow{\text{finite convolutions}}\;
\widehat N_r,\widehat M_r,\widehat Q_r,\widehat\chi_r
\;\xrightarrow{}\;
\widehat J_r,\widehat K_r
\;\xrightarrow{}\;
H^{(2),\mathrm{fast}}_{rs}.
}
\end{equation}

For the anisotropy observables, the same accepted branch is fed into the patchwise spectral extractor:

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}
\;\xrightarrow{\mathcal P_\alpha,\Pi_{\rm fam}}\;
\mathcal H_\alpha^{\rm proj}
\;\xrightarrow{\text{eigensolve}}\;
(\chi_\alpha,m_\alpha^2),
}
\end{equation}

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}+h\chi_\alpha
\;\xrightarrow{\mathcal F_{\rm shell}}\;
g_\alpha
=
\Gamma^{(4)}_{\alpha\alpha\alpha\alpha}(0,0,0,0).
}
\end{equation}

Then the raw moments are

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
W_0=\sum_\alpha N_\alpha,
\qquad
W_2=\sum_\alpha N_\alpha P_2(\hat n\cdot\hat k_\alpha),
\qquad
M_2=\sum_\alpha N_\alpha m_\alpha^2,
\qquad
G_4=\sum_\alpha N_\alpha g_\alpha,
}
\end{equation}
with
\[
N_\alpha=\|\Pi_{\rm fam}\chi_\alpha\|^2.
\]

Finally,

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
m_*^2=\frac{M_2}{W_0},
\qquad
g_{\mathrm{eff}}=\frac{G_4}{W_0},
\qquad
\varepsilon_{\mathrm{lock}}=3\frac{W_2}{W_0},
}
\end{equation}

\begin{equation}
\boxed{
Z_{\rm cub}
=
-\frac{G_4^2W_2}{48\pi W_0^{3/2}M_2^{3/2}}
=
-\frac{g_{\mathrm{eff}}^2}{144\pi m_*^3}\varepsilon_{\mathrm{lock}}.
}
\end{equation}

Thus the entire numerical proof-completion problem is reduced to one accepted branch
\(\Psi_{\mathrm{corr}}\) and one finite common extractor.

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\begin{verbatim}

#
# tect_actual_extractor.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# -*- coding: utf-8 -*-

"""
TECT actual-branch numerical extractor
--------------------------------------

Expected input directory contents:

  Psi_corr.npy            : complex array, shape (3, Nx, Ny, Nz)
  hat_n.npy               : real array, shape (3,)
  patch_centers.npy       : real array, shape (Npatch, 3)

Optional:
  G_list.npy              : real array, shape (NG, 3)
  Phi_A.npy               : complex array, shape (3, Nx, Ny, Nz)
  Phi_E.npy               : complex array, shape (3, Nx, Ny, Nz)
  Phi_O.npy               : complex array, shape (3, Nx, Ny, Nz)
  Pi_fam_matrix.npy       : complex/real array, shape (3, 3)
  config.json             : JSON configuration file

Required backend module:
  residual(Psi, params) -> ndarray same shape as Psi
  shell_free_energy(Psi, params) -> real scalar

Optional backend functions:
  hessian_vec(Psi, v, params) -> ndarray same shape as Psi
  apply_family_projector(Psi, params) -> ndarray same shape as Psi
  branch_solver(delta_vec, params) -> ndarray same shape as Psi
  compute_fast_sector_from_harmonics(barA_G, orbit_harmonics, params) -> dict

Usage example:
  python tect_actual_extractor.py --input ./data --backend ./backend.py

Minimal config.json example:
{
  "Lx": 16.0,
  "Ly": 16.0,
  "Lz": 16.0,
  "q0": 1.0,
  "dq_patch": 0.08,
  "dtheta_patch": 0.35,
  "eps_hess": 1e-6,
  "h_quartic": 5e-4,
  "num_eigs": 6,
  "project_family_in_eigensolve": false,
  "delta_corr": [0.0096, -0.0288, 0.0096]
}

Notes:
- This script is fully executable as long as the backend provides the model-specific residual
  and shell free energy.
- If Phi_A/E/O are absent, the script will try to reconstruct them using backend.branch_solver().
- If G_list.npy is present, frozen shell harmonics \bar{A}_G and orbit harmonics B_G^(r)
  are extracted and saved to disk.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import json
import math
import sys
import traceback
import importlib.util
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional, Tuple, Callable, List

import numpy as np
from numpy.fft import fftn, ifftn, fftfreq
from scipy.sparse.linalg import LinearOperator, eigsh


# ============================================================
# Utility
# ============================================================

def eprint(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> None:
    print(*args, file=sys.stderr, **kwargs)


def load_npy_required(path: Path, name: str) -> np.ndarray:
    f = path / name
    if not f.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Required file not found: {f}")
    arr = np.load(f, allow_pickle=False)
    return arr


def load_npy_optional(path: Path, name: str) -> Optional[np.ndarray]:
    f = path / name
    if not f.exists():
        return None
    return np.load(f, allow_pickle=False)


def load_config(path: Path) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    cfg_path = path / "config.json"
    if not cfg_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Required config file not found: {cfg_path}")
    with open(cfg_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
        cfg = json.load(fh)
    return cfg


def load_backend_module(backend_path: Path):
    if not backend_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Backend module not found: {backend_path}")
    spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("tect_backend", str(backend_path))
    if spec is None or spec.loader is None:
        raise ImportError(f"Failed to load backend module from: {backend_path}")
    mod = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod


def ensure_shape(arr: np.ndarray, shape: Tuple[int, ...], name: str) -> None:
    if arr.shape != shape:
        raise ValueError(f"{name} has shape {arr.shape}, expected {shape}")


def normalize_vector(v: np.ndarray, eps: float = 1e-14) -> np.ndarray:
    nrm = np.linalg.norm(v)
    if nrm < eps:
        raise ValueError("Cannot normalize near-zero vector.")
    return v / nrm


def P2(c: float) -> float:
    return 0.5 * (3.0 * c * c - 1.0)


def pretty_complex(z: complex, digits: int = 8) -> str:
    return f"{z.real:.{digits}e}{z.imag:+.{digits}e}j"


# ============================================================
# k-grid and FFT helpers
# ============================================================

def build_k_axes(Nx: int, Ny: int, Nz: int, Lx: float, Ly: float, Lz: float):
    kx = 2.0 * np.pi * fftfreq(Nx, d=Lx / Nx)
    ky = 2.0 * np.pi * fftfreq(Ny, d=Ly / Ny)
    kz = 2.0 * np.pi * fftfreq(Nz, d=Lz / Nz)
    return kx, ky, kz


def build_kgrid(Nx: int, Ny: int, Nz: int, Lx: float, Ly: float, Lz: float):
    kx, ky, kz = build_k_axes(Nx, Ny, Nz, Lx, Ly, Lz)
    KX, KY, KZ = np.meshgrid(kx, ky, kz, indexing="ij")
    K = np.stack([KX, KY, KZ], axis=0)
    Kmag = np.sqrt(np.sum(K**2, axis=0))
    return K, Kmag, kx, ky, kz


def fft_field(Psi: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    return fftn(Psi, axes=(1, 2, 3))


def ifft_field(Psi_k: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    return ifftn(Psi_k, axes=(1, 2, 3))


def nearest_axis_index(axis: np.ndarray, value: float, tol: float = 1e-9) -> int:
    idx = int(np.argmin(np.abs(axis - value)))
    if abs(axis[idx] - value) > tol:
        raise ValueError(
            f"Could not match reciprocal value {value:.12e} on FFT axis within tol={tol}."
        )
    return idx


def reciprocal_index_from_vector(
    G: np.ndarray,
    kx: np.ndarray,
    ky: np.ndarray,
    kz: np.ndarray,
    tol: float = 1e-9,
) -> Tuple[int, int, int]:
    ix = nearest_axis_index(kx, float(G[0]), tol=tol)
    iy = nearest_axis_index(ky, float(G[1]), tol=tol)
    iz = nearest_axis_index(kz, float(G[2]), tol=tol)
    return ix, iy, iz


# ============================================================
# Family projector handling
# ============================================================

def make_family_projector(
    backend: Any,
    params: Dict[str, Any],
    Pi_fam_matrix: Optional[np.ndarray],
) -> Callable[[np.ndarray], np.ndarray]:
    if hasattr(backend, "apply_family_projector"):
        def apply_family_projector(Psi: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
            out = backend.apply_family_projector(Psi, params)
            if not isinstance(out, np.ndarray):
                raise TypeError("backend.apply_family_projector must return np.ndarray")
            ensure_shape(out, Psi.shape, "apply_family_projector output")
            return out
        return apply_family_projector

    if Pi_fam_matrix is not None:
        if Pi_fam_matrix.shape != (3, 3):
            raise ValueError("Pi_fam_matrix.npy must have shape (3, 3).")

        def apply_family_projector(Psi: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
            return np.einsum("ab,bxyz->axyz", Pi_fam_matrix, Psi)
        return apply_family_projector

    def identity_projector(Psi: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        return Psi

    return identity_projector


# ============================================================
# Frozen shell harmonic extraction
# ============================================================

def extract_shell_harmonics(
    Psi: np.ndarray,
    G_list: np.ndarray,
    kx: np.ndarray,
    ky: np.ndarray,
    kz: np.ndarray,
) -> Dict[Tuple[float, float, float], np.ndarray]:
    if G_list.ndim != 2 or G_list.shape[1] != 3:
        raise ValueError("G_list.npy must have shape (NG, 3).")

    Psi_k = fft_field(Psi) / np.prod(Psi.shape[1:])
    out: Dict[Tuple[float, float, float], np.ndarray] = {}

    for G in G_list:
        idx = reciprocal_index_from_vector(G, kx, ky, kz)
        key = tuple(np.round(G.astype(float), 12))
        out[key] = np.array(Psi_k[:, idx[0], idx[1], idx[2]], copy=True)

    return out


def load_orbit_fields_or_reconstruct(
    input_dir: Path,
    backend: Any,
    params: Dict[str, Any],
    Psi_corr: np.ndarray,
    delta_corr: np.ndarray,
) -> Dict[str, np.ndarray]:
    orbit = {}
    labels = ["A", "E", "O"]
    files = {"A": "Phi_A.npy", "E": "Phi_E.npy", "O": "Phi_O.npy"}

    missing = []
    for lab in labels:
        arr = load_npy_optional(input_dir, files[lab])
        if arr is None:
            missing.append(lab)
        else:
            ensure_shape(arr, Psi_corr.shape, files[lab])
            orbit[lab] = arr

    if not missing:
        return orbit

    if not hasattr(backend, "branch_solver"):
        raise RuntimeError(
            f"Missing orbit fields {missing}, and backend.branch_solver(delta_vec, params) "
            "is not provided."
        )

    h = float(params.get("orbit_fd_step", 1e-4))
    for i, lab in enumerate(labels):
        if lab in orbit:
            continue
        d = np.zeros(3, dtype=float)
        d[i] = h
        Psi_p = backend.branch_solver(delta_corr + d, params)
        Psi_m = backend.branch_solver(delta_corr - d, params)
        if not isinstance(Psi_p, np.ndarray) or not isinstance(Psi_m, np.ndarray):
            raise TypeError("backend.branch_solver must return np.ndarray")
        ensure_shape(Psi_p, Psi_corr.shape, "branch_solver(+)")
        ensure_shape(Psi_m, Psi_corr.shape, "branch_solver(-)")
        orbit[lab] = (Psi_p - Psi_m) / (2.0 * h)

    return orbit


# ============================================================
# Patch projectors
# ============================================================

def patch_mask(
    K: np.ndarray,
    Kmag: np.ndarray,
    q0: float,
    hat_k_alpha: np.ndarray,
    dq: float,
    dtheta: float,
) -> np.ndarray:
    kmag_ok = np.abs(Kmag - q0) < dq
    Khat = K / (Kmag[None, ...] + 1e-14)
    cosang = np.sum(Khat * hat_k_alpha[:, None, None, None], axis=0)
    ang_ok = np.arccos(np.clip(cosang, -1.0, 1.0)) < dtheta
    return kmag_ok & ang_ok


def project_patch(Psi: np.ndarray, mask: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    Psi_k = fft_field(Psi)
    Psi_k = Psi_k * mask[None, ...]
    return ifft_field(Psi_k)


# ============================================================
# Hessian-vector product
# ============================================================

def make_hessian_vec(
    backend: Any,
    params: Dict[str, Any],
) -> Callable[[np.ndarray, np.ndarray], np.ndarray]:
    if hasattr(backend, "hessian_vec"):
        def hessian_vec(Psi: np.ndarray, v: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
            out = backend.hessian_vec(Psi, v, params)
            if not isinstance(out, np.ndarray):
                raise TypeError("backend.hessian_vec must return np.ndarray")
            ensure_shape(out, Psi.shape, "hessian_vec output")
            return out
        return hessian_vec

    if not hasattr(backend, "residual"):
        raise RuntimeError("Backend must provide residual(Psi, params) if hessian_vec is absent.")

    eps_hess = float(params.get("eps_hess", 1e-6))

    def hessian_vec(Psi: np.ndarray, v: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        Rp = backend.residual(Psi + eps_hess * v, params)
        Rm = backend.residual(Psi - eps_hess * v, params)
        if not isinstance(Rp, np.ndarray) or not isinstance(Rm, np.ndarray):
            raise TypeError("backend.residual must return np.ndarray")
        ensure_shape(Rp, Psi.shape, "residual(+)")
        ensure_shape(Rm, Psi.shape, "residual(-)")
        return (Rp - Rm) / (2.0 * eps_hess)

    return hessian_vec


# ============================================================
# Realification for eigensolver
# ============================================================

def flatten_complex_field(Psi: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    re = np.ascontiguousarray(Psi.real).ravel()
    im = np.ascontiguousarray(Psi.imag).ravel()
    return np.concatenate([re, im], axis=0)


def unflatten_complex_field(vec: np.ndarray, shape: Tuple[int, ...]) -> np.ndarray:
    n = int(np.prod(shape))
    re = vec[:n].reshape(shape)
    im = vec[n:].reshape(shape)
    return re + 1j * im


# ============================================================
# Patch mode extraction
# ============================================================

def build_patch_linear_operator(
    Psi_corr: np.ndarray,
    patch_mask_alpha: np.ndarray,
    apply_family_projector: Callable[[np.ndarray], np.ndarray],
    hessian_vec: Callable[[np.ndarray, np.ndarray], np.ndarray],
    strict_project_family: bool,
) -> LinearOperator:
    shape = Psi_corr.shape
    size = 2 * int(np.prod(shape))

    def matvec(x: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        v = unflatten_complex_field(x, shape)
        v = project_patch(v, patch_mask_alpha)
        if strict_project_family:
            v = apply_family_projector(v)
        Hv = hessian_vec(Psi_corr, v)
        Hv = project_patch(Hv, patch_mask_alpha)
        if strict_project_family:
            Hv = apply_family_projector(Hv)
        y = flatten_complex_field(Hv)
        return np.asarray(y, dtype=np.float64)

    return LinearOperator((size, size), matvec=matvec, dtype=np.float64)


def extract_patch_mode(
    Psi_corr: np.ndarray,
    patch_mask_alpha: np.ndarray,
    apply_family_projector: Callable[[np.ndarray], np.ndarray],
    hessian_vec: Callable[[np.ndarray, np.ndarray], np.ndarray],
    num_eigs: int,
    strict_project_family: bool,
) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, float, float]:
    op = build_patch_linear_operator(
        Psi_corr=Psi_corr,
        patch_mask_alpha=patch_mask_alpha,
        apply_family_projector=apply_family_projector,
        hessian_vec=hessian_vec,
        strict_project_family=strict_project_family,
    )

    # 'SM' = smallest magnitude. For realified Hermitian Hessian near the target branch,
    # the desired low patch mode is typically among these modes.
    evals, evecs = eigsh(op, k=num_eigs, which="SM")

    # Prefer the smallest positive mode if present; otherwise fallback to smallest |eval|.
    positive_indices = [i for i, ev in enumerate(evals) if ev > 0.0]
    if positive_indices:
        idx = min(positive_indices, key=lambda i: evals[i])
    else:
        idx = int(np.argmin(np.abs(evals)))

    chi = unflatten_complex_field(evecs[:, idx], Psi_corr.shape)
    chi = project_patch(chi, patch_mask_alpha)

    norm_full = float(np.sqrt(np.sum(np.abs(chi) ** 2).real))
    if norm_full < 1e-14:
        raise RuntimeError("Extracted patch mode has near-zero norm.")
    chi = chi / norm_full

    chi_fam = apply_family_projector(chi)
    Nalpha = float(np.sum(np.abs(chi_fam) ** 2).real / (np.sum(np.abs(chi) ** 2).real + 1e-14))
    m2 = float(evals[idx])

    return chi, m2, Nalpha


# ============================================================
# Quartic coefficient extraction
# ============================================================

def extract_galpha_from_energy(
    Psi_corr: np.ndarray,
    chi_alpha: np.ndarray,
    backend: Any,
    params: Dict[str, Any],
) -> float:
    if not hasattr(backend, "shell_free_energy"):
        raise RuntimeError("Backend must provide shell_free_energy(Psi, params).")

    h = float(params.get("h_quartic", 5e-4))

    def F(t: float) -> float:
        val = backend.shell_free_energy(Psi_corr + t * chi_alpha, params)
        val = float(np.real(val))
        return val

    Fm2 = F(-2.0 * h)
    Fm1 = F(-1.0 * h)
    F0 = F(0.0)
    Fp1 = F(1.0 * h)
    Fp2 = F(2.0 * h)

    fourth_deriv = (Fm2 - 4.0 * Fm1 + 6.0 * F0 - 4.0 * Fp1 + Fp2) / (h ** 4)
    g_alpha = fourth_deriv / 12.0
    return float(g_alpha)


# ============================================================
# Raw moments and effective observables
# ============================================================

def compute_raw_moments(
    hat_n: np.ndarray,
    patch_centers: np.ndarray,
    N_alpha: np.ndarray,
    m_alpha2: np.ndarray,
    g_alpha: np.ndarray,
) -> Tuple[float, float, float, float]:
    W0 = 0.0
    W2 = 0.0
    M2 = 0.0
    G4 = 0.0

    for hk, Nw, m2, g4 in zip(patch_centers, N_alpha, m_alpha2, g_alpha):
        hk = normalize_vector(np.asarray(hk, dtype=float))
        c = float(np.dot(hat_n, hk))
        W0 += float(Nw)
        W2 += float(Nw) * P2(c)
        M2 += float(Nw) * float(m2)
        G4 += float(Nw) * float(g4)

    return W0, W2, M2, G4


def compute_effective_observables(
    W0: float,
    W2: float,
    M2: float,
    G4: float,
) -> Dict[str, float]:
    if W0 <= 0.0:
        raise ValueError(f"W0 must be positive, got {W0}")
    if M2 <= 0.0:
        raise ValueError(f"M2 must be positive, got {M2}")

    mstar2 = M2 / W0
    mstar = math.sqrt(mstar2)
    geff = G4 / W0
    eps_lock = 3.0 * W2 / W0
    Zcub = -(G4 ** 2 * W2) / (48.0 * math.pi * (W0 ** 1.5) * (M2 ** 1.5))

    return {
        "mstar2": mstar2,
        "mstar": mstar,
        "geff": geff,
        "eps_lock": eps_lock,
        "Zcub": Zcub,
    }


# ============================================================
# Optional fast-sector harmonic saver / extractor
# ============================================================

def maybe_extract_frozen_harmonics(
    input_dir: Path,
    output_dir: Path,
    backend: Any,
    params: Dict[str, Any],
    Psi_corr: np.ndarray,
    delta_corr: np.ndarray,
    kx: np.ndarray,
    ky: np.ndarray,
    kz: np.ndarray,
) -> None:
    G_list = load_npy_optional(input_dir, "G_list.npy")
    if G_list is None:
        print("[info] G_list.npy not found; skipping frozen harmonic extraction.")
        return

    barA_G = extract_shell_harmonics(Psi_corr, G_list, kx, ky, kz)
    orbit_fields = load_orbit_fields_or_reconstruct(
        input_dir=input_dir,
        backend=backend,
        params=params,
        Psi_corr=Psi_corr,
        delta_corr=delta_corr,
    )
    orbit_harmonics = {
        lab: extract_shell_harmonics(Phi, G_list, kx, ky, kz)
        for lab, Phi in orbit_fields.items()
    }

    # Save harmonics in a simple NPZ form.
    G_keys = np.array(list(barA_G.keys()), dtype=float)
    barA_vals = np.stack([barA_G[tuple(k)] for k in G_keys], axis=0)
    BA_vals = np.stack([orbit_harmonics["A"][tuple(k)] for k in G_keys], axis=0)
    BE_vals = np.stack([orbit_harmonics["E"][tuple(k)] for k in G_keys], axis=0)
    BO_vals = np.stack([orbit_harmonics["O"][tuple(k)] for k in G_keys], axis=0)

    np.savez(
        output_dir / "frozen_harmonics.npz",
        G_list=G_keys,
        barA_G=barA_vals,
        B_G_A=BA_vals,
        B_G_E=BE_vals,
        B_G_O=BO_vals,
    )
    print(f"[info] Saved frozen harmonics to: {output_dir / 'frozen_harmonics.npz'}")

    # Optional backend-side fast-sector evaluator
    if hasattr(backend, "compute_fast_sector_from_harmonics"):
        fast = backend.compute_fast_sector_from_harmonics(barA_G, orbit_harmonics, params)
        np.save(output_dir / "fast_sector.npy", fast, allow_pickle=True)
        print(f"[info] Saved fast-sector data to: {output_dir / 'fast_sector.npy'}")
    else:
        print("[info] backend.compute_fast_sector_from_harmonics not provided; skipped.")


# ============================================================
# Main extraction pipeline
# ============================================================

def full_actual_branch_extractor(
    input_dir: Path,
    output_dir: Path,
    backend: Any,
    params: Dict[str, Any],
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    Psi_corr = load_npy_required(input_dir, "Psi_corr.npy")
    hat_n = load_npy_required(input_dir, "hat_n.npy").astype(float)
    patch_centers = load_npy_required(input_dir, "patch_centers.npy").astype(float)
    Pi_fam_matrix = load_npy_optional(input_dir, "Pi_fam_matrix.npy")

    if Psi_corr.ndim != 4 or Psi_corr.shape[0] != 3:
        raise ValueError("Psi_corr.npy must have shape (3, Nx, Ny, Nz).")
    if hat_n.shape != (3,):
        raise ValueError("hat_n.npy must have shape (3,).")
    if patch_centers.ndim != 2 or patch_centers.shape[1] != 3:
        raise ValueError("patch_centers.npy must have shape (Npatch, 3).")

    hat_n = normalize_vector(hat_n)

    Nx, Ny, Nz = Psi_corr.shape[1:]
    Lx = float(params["Lx"])
    Ly = float(params["Ly"])
    Lz = float(params["Lz"])
    q0 = float(params["q0"])
    dq_patch = float(params.get("dq_patch", 0.08 * q0))
    dtheta_patch = float(params.get("dtheta_patch", 0.35))
    num_eigs = int(params.get("num_eigs", 6))
    strict_project_family = bool(params.get("project_family_in_eigensolve", False))

    K, Kmag, kx, ky, kz = build_kgrid(Nx, Ny, Nz, Lx, Ly, Lz)
    apply_family_projector = make_family_projector(backend, params, Pi_fam_matrix)
    hessian_vec = make_hessian_vec(backend, params)

    delta_corr = np.asarray(params.get("delta_corr", [0.0096, -0.0288, 0.0096]), dtype=float)

    # Optional frozen harmonic extraction for \bar A_G and orbit harmonics
    maybe_extract_frozen_harmonics(
        input_dir=input_dir,
        output_dir=output_dir,
        backend=backend,
        params=params,
        Psi_corr=Psi_corr,
        delta_corr=delta_corr,
        kx=kx,
        ky=ky,
        kz=kz,
    )

    N_list: List[float] = []
    m2_list: List[float] = []
    g_list: List[float] = []

    for ia, hk in enumerate(patch_centers):
        hk = normalize_vector(np.asarray(hk, dtype=float))
        mask = patch_mask(K, Kmag, q0, hk, dq=dq_patch, dtheta=dtheta_patch)

        chi_alpha, m2, Nalpha = extract_patch_mode(
            Psi_corr=Psi_corr,
            patch_mask_alpha=mask,
            apply_family_projector=apply_family_projector,
            hessian_vec=hessian_vec,
            num_eigs=num_eigs,
            strict_project_family=strict_project_family,
        )
        g_alpha = extract_galpha_from_energy(
            Psi_corr=Psi_corr,
            chi_alpha=chi_alpha,
            backend=backend,
            params=params,
        )

        N_list.append(Nalpha)
        m2_list.append(m2)
        g_list.append(g_alpha)

        print(
            f"[patch {ia:03d}] "
            f"N_alpha={Nalpha:.10e}, "
            f"m_alpha^2={m2:.10e}, "
            f"g_alpha={g_alpha:.10e}"
        )

    N_alpha = np.asarray(N_list, dtype=float)
    m_alpha2 = np.asarray(m2_list, dtype=float)
    g_alpha = np.asarray(g_list, dtype=float)

    W0, W2, M2, G4 = compute_raw_moments(
        hat_n=hat_n,
        patch_centers=patch_centers,
        N_alpha=N_alpha,
        m_alpha2=m_alpha2,
        g_alpha=g_alpha,
    )
    obs = compute_effective_observables(W0=W0, W2=W2, M2=M2, G4=G4)

    results = {
        "N_alpha": N_alpha,
        "m_alpha2": m_alpha2,
        "g_alpha": g_alpha,
        "W0": W0,
        "W2": W2,
        "M2": M2,
        "G4": G4,
        **obs,
    }

    np.savez(output_dir / "actual_branch_results.npz", **results)
    print(f"[info] Saved final results to: {output_dir / 'actual_branch_results.npz'}")

    return results


# ============================================================
# CLI
# ============================================================

def build_argparser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description="TECT actual-branch extractor: Psi_corr -> raw moments -> effective observables"
    )
    p.add_argument(
        "--input",
        required=True,
        type=str,
        help="Input directory containing .npy arrays and config.json",
    )
    p.add_argument(
        "--backend",
        required=True,
        type=str,
        help="Path to backend.py implementing residual() and shell_free_energy()",
    )
    p.add_argument(
        "--output",
        default=None,
        type=str,
        help="Output directory. Default: same as input directory",
    )
    return p


# ============================================================
# Main
# ============================================================

def main() -> None:
    parser = build_argparser()
    args = parser.parse_args()

    input_dir = Path(args.input).expanduser().resolve()
    output_dir = Path(args.output).expanduser().resolve() if args.output else input_dir
    backend_path = Path(args.backend).expanduser().resolve()

    try:
        if not input_dir.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"Input directory does not exist: {input_dir}")
        output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

        params = load_config(input_dir)
        backend = load_backend_module(backend_path)

        # Basic backend validation
        if not hasattr(backend, "residual") and not hasattr(backend, "hessian_vec"):
            raise RuntimeError(
                "Backend must provide at least one of: residual(Psi, params), "
                "hessian_vec(Psi, v, params)"
            )
        if not hasattr(backend, "shell_free_energy"):
            raise RuntimeError("Backend must provide shell_free_energy(Psi, params)")

        print("=" * 72)
        print("TECT actual-branch numerical extractor")
        print("=" * 72)
        print(f"Input directory : {input_dir}")
        print(f"Backend module  : {backend_path}")
        print(f"Output directory: {output_dir}")
        print("-" * 72)

        results = full_actual_branch_extractor(
            input_dir=input_dir,
            output_dir=output_dir,
            backend=backend,
            params=params,
        )

        print("-" * 72)
        print("Final effective observables")
        print("-" * 72)
        print(f"W0               = {results['W0']:.16e}")
        print(f"W2               = {results['W2']:.16e}")
        print(f"M2               = {results['M2']:.16e}")
        print(f"G4               = {results['G4']:.16e}")
        print()
        print(f"m*^2             = {results['mstar2']:.16e}")
        print(f"m*               = {results['mstar']:.16e}")
        print(f"g_eff            = {results['geff']:.16e}")
        print(f"epsilon_lock     = {results['eps_lock']:.16e}")
        print(f"Z_cub            = {results['Zcub']:.16e}")
        print("=" * 72)

    except Exception as exc:
        eprint("=" * 72)
        eprint("ERROR: extraction failed")
        eprint("=" * 72)
        eprint(str(exc))
        eprint("-" * 72)
        traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
    
\end{verbatim}
